I. Amagumbi 
  Uma sibheka imephu sifanele siqiniseleke ukuthi inga. kuphi inyakatho, iningizimu, impumalanga nentshonalanga. Lamagumbi omane yiwona magumbi asemqoka ekhampasi. INDLELA ABANTU ABAHLALA NGAYO

A. Uthungulu-I sifunda Sasogwini.-Isilimo esisemqoka esimila othungulu ngurnoba. Umoba lona utshalwa phakathi kwePort Shepstone ngaseningizimu neSt. Lucia ngasenyakatho. Kuthi ngasekuqhubekeni impela ngasenyakatho kube khona indawana encane eduze komfula uPongolo lapho umoba ukhula kahle kakhulu. Kuwo wonke lomdweshu kamoba kunemishini eminingi egaya umoba. Kuthi-ke lapho umoba lona uhlifizeka kuphume umpe olube selubiliswa kuze kuphume izinhlayiyana zikashukela. Lomdweshu okutshalwa kuwo umoba ukwazi ukwenelisa lonke leli lakithi kuze kube khona insalela ethengiswa kwelaseGreat Britain. 

  Izithelo zezindawo ezinekilayimethi esatropiki zimila kahle kakhulu. Zilungiswa kahle bese zithunyelwa emakethe. Ubhanana ungesinye salezi zithelo esande kakhulu. Ezinye-ke izithelo zalolu hlobo ezitshalwayo nazo, uphayinaphu, umango kanye nophopho. 

  ABantu batshala futhi nommbila. Kuhambe kuba nezivande-ke futhi ezigojananeni lapho kutshalwa khona irayisi. AmaNdiya kawacushwa ngerayisi, yisilimo sawo esisemqoka. 

  Umsebenzi wezimayini awubalulekile kakhulu. Kodwake kukhona izindimbane zeilmenite eduze noMgababa ngasoGwini oluseNingizimu. I-ilmenite lena-ke isetshenziselwa ekwakheni opende nezinhlobo ezithile zest iii. 

  Idolobha elikhulu kunawo wonke eNatal iDurban ngoba inetheku elinomsebenzi omningi kakhulu. Futhi [eli theku lisemqoka kunawo wonke amanye kulelizwe. IDurban inamafektri amaningi, okuningt lawo lenza izinto eziningi ngezimpahla ezithunyelwa ziphume emazweni aphesheya. Sizobuye sande nalokhu esahlukweni esilandelayo. Ezinye izindawo zemisebenzi othungulu zakha futhi amakhemikheli nomanyolo, njengaseMbogintwini. Kwenziwa izinhlobo eziningi zamaphepha eMandeni, eFelixton, kanye nasemaphethelweni eDurban.   K wakuhamba kuhambe sibone ujantshi wesitimela uqonde entshonalanga udabula ezabelweni. Isitimela lesi sisemqoka empilweni yabantu ngoba yisona sithwala nokudla sikulethe ezitolo kanti nabanye abantu bagibela sona lapho beya edolobheni beyosebenza.

  Kwathi sekuphele ama-awa amabili sisukile ePietermaritzburg safmyelela emkhakheni wezolimo eUnderberg. Lapha sayibonela eduze iDrakensberg. Ukuba sasize ngesitimela uhambo lwethu lolu esasiluhambe ngemoto lwaluyophindwa kane. Ujantshi wesitimela uzungeza ugege uthathele ugudle izintaba umuntu aze akhathale. 
  IUnderberg isendaweni lapho abalirni benza izinto ezingxube: bayalima, futhi bafuye ngoba ubusika bubanda kakhulu ukuthi ikhona into engamila khona. Ukufuya yikhona kusemqoka. Iningi lalezi zinkomo lalilihle impela futhi lathengwa ngentengo ephezulu.   Nezirnvu zifuna ukuqashelwa kakhulu. Nazo kuhamba zidijwe emadiphini amade amancane ayirnicingwana.

Kufanele futhi kuthi ehlobo, ikakhulukazi uma lishlsa libuye line, zibhekwe njalo ngezikhathi ezithize zisuswe izibungu. Mhlawumbe okuyiwona msebenzi onqamula iqolo kunayo yonke eminye, ukujova leyo naleyomvu emhlambini, ukuze zivikeleke ezifeni eziningi eziphatha izimvu. 
  Kwathi emaphethelweni elokishi sabona ifektri likashizi lapho abalirni abaningi endaweni belusa khona ubisi Iwabo. Lelifektri lakhiwe ngesu lokubambisana. Kuphuma umhlambi wamaloli nsukuzonke uyolanda ubisi kubalimi abaningi. 
Esiteshini sabona inqwaba yamasaka amazambane. 
Phela amazambane avuma kahle kakhulu Ezimfundeni Zotshani Ezingasentshonalanga. Mningi impela umsebenzi lapho amazambane esakhuliswa nalapho esembiwa. Kodwa-ke omunye umsebenzi ubuye wenziwe lula ngokuba abalimi basebenzise imishini ekuwahlwanyeleni nasekuwavuneni. 
  Sathi lapho sikhuluma nomlimi esiteshini sathola ukuthi utshani buvamiswe ukushiswa ebusika ukllze kumile utshani obusha masinyane idle imfuyo entwasahlobo. Abalimi baye baqaphele ukuthi utshani babushisa kuphela emva kokuba izulu kade linile ukuze umhlabathi ungalimazeki ukushisa komlilo. Akusiyo inhlakanipho ukushisa phakathi kobusika ngoba ngaleso sikhathi yonke into yomile. 
  Kwathi lapho sesiphindela ePietermaritzburg sakhweza urnlisa owayephuma khona Ezimfundeni Zotshani Ezingasentshonalanga ngokuyela ngasenyakatho eduze kwaseBergville. Wasitshela ukuthi isifunda sakubo sasifana zikishi nesifunda saseUnderberg. Kukhona ifektri futhi naseBergville elisebenza ubisi, noma-ke lona lingenzi shizi, kodwa-ke lenza ubisi lwamathini, ikhondensi. Umlisa lona wasitshela ukuthi iDrakensberg eBergville ihuha abeLungu abaningi abasuka emadolobheni bavakashele khona, bakhwele nezintaba, bagibele, bashaywe nangurnoya omnandi opholile. Kulo lonke ugoma lwezintaba kusukela eUnderberg kuya ngasekusondeleni neBergville kukhona amahotela namapulazi lapho izivakashi ziyaye zifikele khona ziphathwe kahle.

A. Jnkangala. 
  Isitshalo esisemqoka Enkangala ku1alimi. baBantu nabeLungu. ngummbila. Ummbila uthanda izimvula ezina ehlobo. ngoba utshalwa entwasahlobo iqala nje, bese uvunwa ekupheleni kwehlobo. lwanakazanyana emhlabathini. Okllnye fllthi okutshalwayo Enkangala. ngamazambane atshalwa ikakhulukazi ngasempumalanga eduze kwaseBethal.

B. Jzimfunda Eziphakathi 

  Utshani namahlathi Ezimfunda Eziphakathi yikhona kuyidlelo elihle lezinkomo. Ziningi izinkomo ezifuywe lapho ngabalimi ukuze kutholakale inyama. Amapulazi okufuyelwa kuwona izinkomo makhulu abanzi ukuze izinkomo zithole ukudla okwanele ngisho ebusika utshani sebuphaphathekile baba mpofana boma baba luqhwememe. yestili esetshenziswa ekwakheni ihedigiya (isaklllWO esiphezu komgodi wemayini) yemayini engaphezu kwalowo nalowo mgodi wemayini. Efektri eliseduze singabona onjiniyela besebenza benza amaphampu abanzi asetshenziswa ngaphansi ezimayini ukumpompa izigicli ngezigidi zamalitha amanzi alethwe ngaphezulu. Lamanzi ngasuke engene afinineka edwaleni aye aphumela ezindaweni okusetshenzelwa kuzona ezimayini. 
  Uma sisuka kulesi sifuncla esingasempumalanga, sinqamula siqonda eningizimu yezindawo zemisebenzi, sifika emafektri enza amafenisha nezingubo. Njengoba kunenani elikhulu kangaka labantu abahlala eJ ohannesburg nakwamanye amadolobha eWitwatersrand, abenzi bezingubo namafenisha kabantuli ukuthi lezi zinto zizothengwa ngubani. 
  Ngasentshonalanga sithola indawo eyaziwa ngokuthi Industria okuwukuthi Yisifunda Semisebenzi Yohwebo. Lendawo isemaphethelweni edolobha, inamafektri amaningi. Lamafektri enza izimpahla ezahlukene, ezinye zazo yizimpahla ze-elektriki, zemetheli, yimishini nezingubo zokugqoka. Ngisho nasekuyeleni ngasentshonalanga amafektri ayanda. Lapha kukhona ifektri elikhulu elibonakala kalula elenza amaphayiphi amakhulu ngosimende eduze komgwaqo. 
  Amafektri kawakhiwe phakathi eJohannesburg kuphela. Kunamaningi aseWitwatersrand, eGermiston naseBenoni ikakhulu. Ngasenyakatho yaseJohannesburg kukhona ifektri elikhulu lekhemikheli eModderfontein. Lelifektri liguqula izindimbane zikadalimede zilungiselelwe ukusetshenziswa ezimayini. 
  Emva kokucwaningisisa amafektri ngaphakathi nangaphandle kwaseJohannesburg, sifikelwa umqondo wokuthi amaningi alamafektri akhona nje ngoba kukhona izimayini zegolide, ngoba imayini yanamhlanje isidinga izinhlobo eziningi zemishini. Kanti futhi kudingeka izingubo zokugqoka kanye nezinye izinto zokusebenza izisebenzi. Ngaphandle kwezimayini, iJohannesburg yayingeke nje nempela ibe nabantu abedlule esigidini abadinga izingubo zokugqoka, ifenisha, izimpahla zeelektriki, nezemetheli onke amalanga empilweni yaboo

ISAHLUKO 15 
UHAMBO OLUBHEKE EMFUNDENI EPHAKATHI 
  Imfunda Ephakathi ingasenyakatho yeNkangala eTransvaal. Njengoba-ke Imfunda Ephakathi kayiphakeme yon a kakhulu ukusukela olwandle, ehlobo khona kuyashisa irnpela, kanti ebusika futhi kukhudumele kunasenkangala. Okuzimilela ngokwemvelo laphaya futhi kwehlukile, kwaziwa ngelokuthi yiHlanze-ingxubevange yotshani, yezihlahlana ezibhashile nezihlahla zempela ezikhulile. 
  Sasuka ekhaya eliseMe,!dowlands Bantu Township ngasemaphethelweni angaseningizimu e] ohannesburg, saqonda enyakatho sihamba ngomgwaqo oya ePretoria, siphikelele eMessina kude Ie ngasenyakatho nephrovinsi. Cishe amakhilomitha ali-14 ngasenyakatho Pretoria sasha yeka sadabula eOnderstepoort, lapho kukhona indawo yabacwaningi besayensi abasebenza nzima befuna ukuthola imithi yokwelapha izifo ezimvini, ezinkomeni nasemahashini. 
Ngokuyela ngasenyakatho sedlula' iBon' Accord Dam. 
Eduze kwayo sabona abanye abalimi besebenza benisela amasirnu abo ngenkasa, amanzi bewadonsa khona edamini. Maningi amadamu angasekupheleni kweMfunda Ephakathi ngaseningizimu. Idamu elaziwa kakhulu ngelibizwa ngokuthiwa yiHartebeestpoort Dam, elingasentshonalanga nePretoria. Amanzi asuka kulamadamu asiza abalimi ekutshaleni ukolo ebusika nogwayi ehlobo. 
  Sahamba amakhilomitha ngamakhilomitha ngomgwaqo owawuqondile udabula emathafeni amile utshani nezihlahlana zehlanze ezibhashile ezinameva. Sasihamba sihambe sizithele emhlambini omuhle wezinkomo zenyama, imvamisa ezibizwa ngokuthiwa ngamaHumpbacked Africanders. Yilapho sezwa khona nokuthi Imfunda Ephakathi ingenye yezimfunda ezisemqoka lapho kutholakala khona inyama.

  Yithi labayana-ke sidabula endaweni okuthiwa yiSpringhok Flats, lapho sabona amasimu amaningi ommbila namantongomani. Abanye abalimi lapho babetshale izilimo nezimbali ukuze lokhu bakuthengise ePretoria naseJohannesburg.

  ISIVIVINYO .MAYELANA NEMIKHIQIZO YOHWEBO YENDAWO ENGENAYO ETRANS. 
VAAL 
  Ukudla okusetshenziswa eTransvaal imvamisa yakho kukhiqizwa kuyiphrovinsi. Kufanele wazi ukuthi ummbila omningi utshalwaphi-umkhakha osemqoka wommbila eSouth Africa! Ake usho ukuthi ingxenye kakolo osetshenziswa eTransvaal uphurnaphi. Enye ingxenye ithwalwa ngesitimela isuswa e-Eastern Orange Free State nasePhrovinsi yaseCape. lyiphi ingxenye yephrovinsi efunzela ngezithelo ezisathrophiki eziningi? 
  ITransvaal inamafektri amaningi okwedlulele wonke amanye amaphrovinsi. Iningi lalamafektri lingaseWitwatersrand. Umkhakha lona ubuye uxhumeleleke uqonde ngaseningizimu uphikelele eVereeniging bese kuba khona omunye urnkhakha oxhumelele ngasenyakatho uphikelele ePretoria. K unamafektri asebenzisa izimpahla zendawo eziluhlaza noma ezingakasetshenziswa. Kulawo kukhona akha imikhiqizo yokudla, njengebhotela noshizi kanye necornflakes eyenziwa ngommbila. Amanye njalo asebenza ngomkhando wensimbi ophuma eThabazimbi Emfundeni Ephakathi naseNyakatho Cape, kanye nengxube yamalahle akuleyo ndawo kanye namalahle aphuma eNyakatho::Natal ukuze enze insimbi nestili. Amanye-ke njalo enza izimpahla zokusebenza emapulazini kanye nemishini yakhona. Yimaphi amanye amaminareli ambiwa asetshenzwe eTransvaal? Amafektri ogwayi anenqwaba yogwayi ongakasetshenzwa enza ngawo usikilidi. Kambe uthi ungasho nje ukuthi ugwayi lona utshalwaphi? 
  Kukhona eminye imikhiqizo iTransvaal eyithola kwezinye izingxenye zaseSouth Africa noma emazweni aphesheya. Ake silinganise nje, abantu abahlala eTransvaal baphuza itiye nekhofi, kokubili lokhu kuthunyelwa kususwe emazweni aphesheya. Iningi likashukela eliphuzwa nalezi ziphuzo liphurna eNatal. Noma ekhona amafektri ayingcosana asebenza ngokotini nangovolo eRand, kawakwazi ukumelana nendlela izingubo ezidingeka ngayo, ngakho iningi lalokhu kuthunyelwa kususwe eBritain, eAmerica nase-Europe.

  Bonke abantu bayazakhela izindlu noma bazifunele bona mathupha izindawo zokukhose:a bavikele iZ1l1u baphephe nasezitheni zabo. 
Ezabelweni eSol1th Africa kl1namaqhugwane amaningi. 
Imvamisa amaqhugwane lawa akhiwe kahle kakhl1lu. Izindonga zingakhiwa ngamasoyi, kanti kwezinye izindawo, ikakhulukazi lapho kutholakala khona izingodo, zakhiwa ngezigxobo eziqondile eziphicwa ngosaba, bese kuhuqwa-ke ngodaka, bese kubuye kuhuqwe kucolisiswe-ke manje. Phezulu kufulelwa ngotshani. Ngesinye isikhathi eZululand yonke indlu imiswa ibe yindilinga, bese yonke ifulelwa imbozeke utshani. Lamaqhugwana aphaswa yizinsika ngaphakathi. 
  Emalokishini abantu njengaseMeadowlands (eduze kwase]ohannesburg) eGarankuwa (eduze kwasePretoria), KwaMashu (eduze kwaseDurban) nasell1bali (eduze kwasePietermaritzburg) sekwakhiwe izink1l1ungwane ngezinkulungwane zamakhaya aqinile. Izindonga zakhiwe

ngezitini noma ngamabhulokwe kasemende. Phezult. kufulelwe ngeasbhestos noma ngothayela (uzinki) ... Amafasitela ngawensimbi kanti neminyango ngeyensimbi. Yileyo naleyondlu inamakamelo ambalwa.   Emadolobheni amakhulu kwakhiwa amahostela okuhlala abantu abaNsundu. Lapha izisebenzi zinokuhlala zilaIe ngesikhathi zisebenza edolobheni. Ezinye zalezi zindawo, amafektri nezimayini, ake silinganise nje ngezimayini zegolide, sezakha izindlu ezinkulu ezibizwa ngokuthiwa yizinkomponi. Lezi zindlu zihlala izisebenzi eziNsundu.

Bonke abantu abahlala kulezo zingxenye sebabuyiselwa ndawonye kulamalokishi amasha asebakhelwa wona. Ukuhlela izindawo zokuhlala ngalendlela kwenza kube lula ukulungiselela izindawo zamadlelo namasimu.

  Abalimi abaningi abaNsundu sebelufundile manje usizo lokungatshali izilimo ezifanayo minyaka yonke. Sebesifundile nesidingo sokonga umhlabathi. Sebelufundile nosizo lomquba nomanyolo. ZABAKHA IMIGWAQO 
IposI. Kudala impela endulo, abantu babenobunzima obukhulu uma behambisa imibiko emazweni akude. Kodwa-ke namhlanje sesikwazi ukuthumela incwadi isuke kwelinye izwe iye kwelinye kodwa sibe sikhokhe amasenti ayingcosana nje kuphela. Lomsebenzi-ke wenziwa liposi. Iposi linoMkhulu walo ePretoria, namahovisi-ke amaningi amancane ahamba eba sezindaweni ngezindawo kuleli Iakithi. Noma izindlu ezisetshenziswa ngabeposi emadolobheni amakhulu zizinkulu kakhulu kunalezo ezisemalokishini noma ezindaweni ezincane nnke amaposi anikeza abantu usizo. Akesithi-ke siva: kashele eposini, akesicabange futhi ukuthi zinto zini esizifica lapho. 
  K~thi ~Ja singena ep?s.ini sibone ikhawunta. Laphake slkwazl ukuthenga lZltembu ukuze sizinamathisele ezincwa~ni zethu nasemaphaseleni ethu ngaphambi kokuba slpose. Uma singenalo iqiniso ukuthi kudingeka izitembu zamalini ephaseleni, siyaye sicele lona ongemuva kwekhawunta ukuba asikalele isisindo sayo. Kuthi-ke angayikala bese esitshela ukuthi asithenge izitembu zamalini. 
. .Kw~linye icala lekhawunta yilapho sithwnela khona lzmg.cmg? (zok"Ubhalw:;). Lez! zingcingo zithunyelwa ngezmgcmgo oyaye uzlbone eZlgxotsheni eduze kwemigwaqo. f 
  Ngakwelinye icala futhi lekhawunta sithenga amaposoda. Uma umuntu efuna ukuthumela imali ngeposi, indlela ephephile yokuthumela ukuthenga iposoda efike ishintshwe phambili. Ukuthumela imali eyisiliva, umuntu ayifake emvilophini, kunengozi ngoba ihamba ihambe iyidabule imvilophi bese iputshuka ilahleka. 
  Eposini futhi kugcinwa imali. Kuyilisu elingcono kakhulu ukugcina imali yethu eposini kunokuyibeka lapho inokwebiwa khona. 
  Ngasekungeneni ngomnyango ongaphambili eposini siyaye sibone uklele lwamabhokisi amancanyana acwebezelayo. Lamabhokisana aqhashwa ngabantu abahlala ezindaweni lapho iposi lingasiwa khona njengoba kwenziwa kwezinye izindawo. Yilelo nalelo bhokisi linenamba. Uma umuntu eqhasha ibhokisi elingunamba II, ikheli lakhe-ke libe selibhalwa kanjena: P.O. Box 11 kulelo posi ephuma kulona. Umqhashi unikwa futhi ukhiye walelobhokisi ukuze iposi lakhe alilande noma ngasikhathi sini asithandayo. 
  Ngaphandle kwaseposini sibona amabhokisana abomvu lapho abantu bekhalakathisela izincwadi khona. Lapha kulamabhokisi kuyaye kube khona izixebeledwana ezicwebezelayo ezibhalwa isikhathi esisitshela ukuthi iposi kulelo bhokisana lizoqoqwa nini, liyohlungwa lilungiselelewe ukufakwa esitimeleni. 
ISITESHI SEZITIMELA 
  Noma ngubani ongenayo imoto indlela elula ukuba ahambe yisitimela. Akuyizo zonke izitimela ezithwala abantu. Ezinye zithwala izilwane, imikhiqizo yabalimi, amalahle, imikhando yensimbi esaxubene netshe, izinsimbi ezisetshenziswa ngabalimi, nokunye. 
  Ihovisi lokuqala esiyaye silibone lapho sifika esiteshini yilapho kuthathwa khona amathikithi. Lapha-ke sithenga amathikithi ezindawo lapho siya khona. Umuntu angelokothe akhwele isitimela engalithathanga ithikithi lakhona. 
  Bese siqhubeka-ke siya eplatifomu. eduz~ kwal~pho izitimela zima khona ukuze abantu bakwazl ukuglbela kahle futhi behle kahle. Eplatifomu kukhona ibhodi elikhulu elibhalwe igama lesiteshi. 
102 
  Eziteshini ezinkulu kukhona izinto eziyaye zenziwe ukuze lube mnandi uhambo lwalabo abasuke begibele noma bezogibela izitimela. Ake silinganise ngesitolo nje lapho kuthengiswa khona amaphephandaba, omagazini nezincwadi zokufunda. Kuvamisa futhi ukuthi duze nje kube khona ithilomu elithengisa amaphayi neziphuzo ezibandayo. 
  Kuyaye kuthi lapho isitimela sifika esiteshini umuntu abone ubuphithiphithi. Iminyango ivuleka ivaleke lapho abantu bengena bephuma, ophotha bagquba izinqodlana zabo baqonde emuva enqoleni ethwele izimpahla. Ubona abangani bevalelisana bexhawulana. Uzwe insimbi ikhala, ubone ugadi ephakamisa iduku eliluhlaza, ubone isitimela sithi gexe, yiso lesiya sinyelela, sishishibala sihamba. 
  Iziteshi ezingena ojantshi bephuma macala onke zinamabhokisana eziboniso lapho lowo ophethe edonsa izigwadlulo ezibonakalisa amasigneli kude buduze nojantshi besitimela. Ngalendlela-ke lowo ophethe uyakwazi ukllmisa isitimela sisekude singakafinyeleli euuaweni lapho besingatholana nesinye bese zingqubllzana. Uma kufanele ukuba ujantshi uhambe uhambe wehlukane kabili, uphambuke kwenziwa esinye isipolo esincane esiphambukayo ukuze izitimela zikwazi ukuhamba ngendlela leyo efunekayo. Ngomunye umsebenzi-ke lowo {uthi kulowo osebhokisaneni lamasigneli. N gokuba athinte isigwadlulo okuyisona sona uyakwazi ukwenza isitimela silandele isipolo esifanele. Ngllyena muntu onomsebenzi osemqoka kakhulu. 
  Kllfanele ukuthi sikhona isiteshi sezitimela eduze nalapho uhlala khona. Zingaki izinto kulezi esezibaliwe lapha ezikhona esiteshini sakini? Qaphela. Ungabohamba uyabule weqana nojantshi. Minyaka yonke abantu bashaywa yisitimela bafe.

gqoka, izimpahlanokudlaesingeze sazitshalela khona thina. 
  Izitolo zangaphandle ziyizindawo ezinedumela elikhulu, noma-ke iningi lazo kuyaye kube yin dIu eyodwa nje enamafasitela amakhulu lapho kuyaye kubekwe khona izimpahla ukuze bazibone kahle abantu. Iningi lezitolo lakhiwe eduze kwezindawo zaBantu. Abanini balezi zitolo-ke bathenga bagcwalise ezitolo zonke izinto ezingahle zidingakale. 
  Ake siye kwesinye salezi zitolo. Phandle laphaya sithola ltkuthi kunamahashi, iminyuzi nezimbongolo. Lezi zilwane ziboshelwe ezihlahleni zendlulamithi. Ezinye zalezi zilwane zilethe uvolo, nezikhumba, okuphuma ezindaweni zaBantu, ukuba kuzothengiswa lapha esitolo. Ngalemali-ke abathengisi laba bathenga ukudla, izinguho zokugqoka, izingubo zokulala kanye nemithi. 
  Phakathi lapha esitolo sithola ukuthi umninisitolo nabasizi bakhe basebenza nje impela bathe nqi ngoba nakhu kukhona iqembu elikhulu elifuna ukuthenga. Sibona kwelinye igosi laphaya enhla umnumzane osengwevu ekhanda ethenga isaka lommbila. Kanti ezansi ngakwelinye igosi kumi uklele Iwabadala nabancane luphethe amabhodlela, lwethelwa uphalafini osedilamini elikhulu. Phela uphalafmi lona kukhanyiswa ngawo izibani emakhaya amaningi asemaphandleni. 
  Ngemuva kwekhawunta-ke kunamashalofu atakwe kahle amabhele ezindwangu ezinemibala egqamile. Kuleli eala-ke sekumi iqembu labesifazane abafuna ukuthenga okokwembatha, lidonswa yilemibala yalendwangu. Phoke abantu besifazane bohlanga oluNsundu baqaphelisisa kakhulu uma bethenga, indwangu bayibukele eduze hefuna ukuyizwa nangesandla ukuthi iyohlala isikllathi eside yini. Ngemuva kwalaba abacubungulana nezindwangu, kumi indoda yomSuthu, iyamamatheka ikhombisa abangani bayo ingubo yayo yokulala emagqabhagqabha esal1lla kuyithenga. 
  Kukhona uhlangothi lapha esitolo olusetshenziselwa izingubo zokugqoka kuphela. Sibona kulenga lapha phezulu kusilingi amabhuzi. Kwamanye amashaJofu kukhona inqwaba yamayembe, amabhulukwe, amabhantshi. izigqoko, amabhalede kanye namakapisi. 
104 
  Njengoba iningi Ialaba bantu lihlala kude nodokotela, kuyamsiza umnini sitolo ukuba kube khona akwaziyo mayelana nemithi yezifana ezincane, bese eyithumela ayithengise khona esitolo sakhe. Ngakwelinye icala sibona amabhodlela amaphilisi ekhanda, amaphilisi esisu, imithi yokukllwehlela, kanye namanye amafutha nokhilimu kubekwe emashalofini. 
  KakusikllO ukuthi zonke izimpahla zibekwa emashalofini. Laphaya ph ansi ngakwelinye igosi khona phakathi esitolo kumi amabhodwe nogalaza kanye namaphaphasi amaningi ahamba ehluka ngobukhulu. 
  Okuyiyona ngxenye yesitolo ehlala izungezwe ngabantu abaningi, yilena ethengisa ukudla. Lapho sibona othengisayo esebenza eshesha, ethengisa inyama esemathinini, ujamu, ushukela, impuphu, ubhontshisi netiye. Uthuka nje esitholile isikhathi sokuphumula. 
  Kuyilapho izitolo emadolobheni zivamise ukuthengisa uhlobo olulodwa lwempahla, njengefenisha, ngemithi, ngezingubo, ngokudliwayo, izitolo zasemaphandleni zona kufanele zizame ukufaka esitolo konke lokho okungadingwa ngabathengi. Ngenxa yokuthi izitolo zasemaphandleni zinakho konke-ke, ngaphandle kwezinto esezibaliwe, sasisenokuthenga lokhu okulandelayo futhi uma sithanda: izipeletu, imiphini yamapiki namakhuba ezandla, amapuleti, imimese, izinkinobho, izincwadi, amapeni kanye nezinto zezingane zokudlala-eqinisweni nje, ngamafuphi, laphaya umuntu unokuthola konke akudingayo empilweni yakhe. 
IZINDLU ZABAKHA IMIGWAQO 
  Imigwaqo isemqoka kakhulu empilweni yalowo nalowo okuleli laseSouth Africa, ngakho kufanele-ke kakhulu ukuba imigwaqo yethu ibe sesimweni esincomekayo, ihlale ilungiswa njalo. Kwesinye isikhathi futhi kuyaye kudingeke ukuba kwakhiwe imigwaqo emisha. 
  Ngubani-ke owenza wonke lomsebenzi? Yileyo naleyo Phrovinsi inoMnyango obhekene nemigwaqo okuyiwona ufeza lomsebenzi. Emalokishini amaningi owaziyo mhlawumbe uyaye uzibone izindlu zalabo abakha imigwaqo. 
  Izindlu lezi zivamise ukuba zibe ningi, kanti ezinye zingamakhaya nje impela abanye balabo abasebenza

84. 
emigwaqeni. Eziningi zalezi zindlu zakhiwa ngohlobo lwebhodi oluthile, noma ngohlobo lokhuni oluthile, ukuze kube lula ukuzithwala zisuke kwenye indawo ziye kwenye. Ziyaye zithuthwe uma usuphelile umsebenzi kuleyo ndawo ebilungiselwa umgwaqo. 
  Lapha emabaleni alapha esikhumlweni sabakha imigwaqo, umuntu ufiea imishini eminingi. Ezinsukwini zakuqala kwakulukhuni ukwenza imigwaqo ngoba umsebenz! om?ingi wawenziwa ngezandla.   Abanye ogandaganda siyaye sibabone bethwele umhlabathi bewus~a kwenye indawo bewusa kwenye, ulayishwe entwem ethwalayo exhunyelelwe khona ngemuva kukagandaganda. Kuyaye kuthi ngesikhathi ugandaganda uhamba, umshayeli avule ingaphansi lalento ethwalayo. Ngesikhathi uhamba-ke ugandaganda, umhlabathi. uyahwayeka ungen.e futhi kuyo lento ethwalayo. KUthl lapho umhlabathl usugewele, umshayeli abese evala, ashayele ugandaganda awuqondise lapho lomhlabathi kufanele uthululelwe khona. Ufika futhi laphaya phambili avule ingaphansi lalento ethwalayo bese kuhuza kuphuma umhlabathi. 
  Eminye imishini ekhona emikhulu isebenza njengamafoshela anamandla amakhulu. Lezi zikhevezi ezimise okwamafoshela zisebenza ngomshini, zikwazi ukuthatha ngasikhathi sinye umhlabathi omkhulu. Zinanemihlathi emikhulu ekwazi ukungena emhlabathini igebhule kakhulu kulayishwe elolini. Lokhu kwenzeka kahle ngoba isikhevezi lesi sixhunyeleJwe ensimbini eyistili ende, esangalo. ijikize kahle, ifinyelele nangakwelinye ieala lomgwaqo. 
  Ngakwelinye igosi lapha esikhumulweni sezimpahla zokusebenza emgwaqeni, kukhona amalori amakhulu anamathangi ngemuva. Lamalori-ke aehela amanzi emigwaqeni ukuze kuthibeke izintuli lapho kusasetshenzwa kuphuquzwa khona kakhulu. Amanye alamalori alanda amanzi aphuzwa yizisebenzi ezisebenza khona lapha emgwaqeni ngoba umsebenzi wasemgwaqeni uyomisana, ikakhulukazi uma kushisa. 
  Eduze kwalamalori aehela amanzi kwakukhona amarola amakhulu ezinsimbi angadonswa ngugandaganda kuphela. K wesinye isikhathi iba mibili imishini, ibe nerola ph.ambili. nelinye n~emuva.   Kuzo izikhumulo zemigwaqo lezi kukhona futhi udibi nje lwamalori. Asetshenziselwa izinto ezehlukene amalori lawa. Amanye awo asebenza ukuthutha izisebenzi ekusenikakhulunantambama kakhulu lapha ziya nalaphasezibuya emsebenzini. Lemishini inosizo olukhulu. Iyaye isetshenziswe ekukhipheni amanzi okuke kwenzeke abe luhlupho raphe kwenziwa imigwaqo emisha. Lemishini inamashubhu erabha. ISAHLUKO 2 ISIZWE-l 
  Kusobala ukuthi isizwe saqala ngokuba kusondelane amaqoqo amancane abantu ababenokhokho oyedwa. Kodwa-ke lamaqoqo ahlangana nabanye futhi, mhlawumbe inhloso kuyikulwa nesitha esithile esasibakhathaza bonke; noma-ke mhlawumbe futhi bahlanganiswa uthando lokwakhelana. 
  Wonke-ke lamaqoqo ayekhuluma ulimi olufanayo, enamasiko afanayo, avumelana futhi ukukhonza in kosi eyodwa. Ngamanye amazwi manje base beyisizwe. 
  Nakwezinye izindawo futhi ezinye izizwe zaqambeka kanjena. 
  Yileso naleso sizwe sasihlala engxenyeni yezwe esasithi ngeyalo. Isizwe sasitshala sivuna ukudla emasimini, seluse izinkomo nezimbuzi, sizakhele nezindlu zokuhlala. Sasiganiselana, kuzalwe izingane. Ngakwelinye icala abadala besizwe babefa. 
  Inkosi kwakunguyena muntu owayehlonishwa kunabo bonke. Izwi lenkosi lalingeqiwa muntu futhi lingathathwa njengeze. Umuzi wenkosi-ke kanye nezingane zenkosi babenesikhundla esibalulekile esizweni. 
  Amanye amakhosi ayenamandla ekwazi ukulwa ngamabutho awo ehlule amanye amakhosi ayakhelene nawo. Uma sesihluliwe-ke lesi esinye isizwe, bese siphoqelelwai kanye nenkosi yaso, ukuba sithele sikhonze kulenkos, 
112 
enqobile. Umbuso kaDingiswayo-ke wawakheke kanjalo, wagcina eseyinkosi enkulu. Kodwa-ke emva kwakhe kwabusa uShaka, .owaba mkhulu ngokwedlulele ngisho uDingiswayo uqobo. Eqinisweni uShaka waphoqelela izizwe eziningi ukuba zibuswe nguyena. 
  Kuleso naleso sizwe abantu babehlukaniswe ngezindlu noma ngemizi. AbeNguni namaThonga ngisho nanamhlanje bayakhe ngokugqagqana imizi yabo endaweni yesizwe. Yilowo nalowo muzi imvamisa wakhelwa ngasekwehleleni kwegquma, noma esigodini, eduze komthombo wamarizi noma komfula. Eduze kwalowo nalowo muzi kukhona amasimu nezivande. Izinkomo, izimbuzi nezimvu zemizi eyahlukene kweluka ndawonye. 
  Abantu abavamise ukuhlala emzini owodwa yindoda (umnllmzane), yinkosikazi yakhe noma ngamakhosikazi akhe, yizingane kanye nezihlobo zakhe. 
  AbeSllthu bona imizi yabo imvamisa bayakha bayisondelanise bese kufana nelokishi. Kulelo nalelo lokishi-ke kukhona indawo okllh1anganelwa kuyo ebizwa ngokuthiwayiKhotla, lapho amadoda asekhulile ehlanganela khona ukuze axoxe izindaba zomkhandlu. 
  Kuzo zonke izizwe eziNsundu umuntu owayenamandla enele llkuthi aganwe ngamakhosikazi amaningi wayevunyelwa. Eqinisweni, umnumzane owayenamakhosikazi amaningi wayehawukeleka futhi etuswa. 
  Kodwa-ke ezikhathini zanamhlanje leli siko seliya ngokuphela. Isizathu salokhu yingoba imfundiso yobuKrestu ingavumelani naleli siko. Esinye isizathu-ke ukuthi izindleko zelobolo seziphezulu, kanti nezokondla amakhosikazi amaningi nezingane zawo sezaba phezulu. 
UMUZI WOMNGUNI 
  Umuzi wempela woMnguni, ezinsukwini eziphambili, wawunesibaya phakathi nendawo, bese kuba ngamaqhugwane-ke azungeze isibaya. Ngaphandle kwakho konkeke lokhu kwakuba nothango olunameva olucinene. Kwakuba khona intuba eyodwa engenela kulolu thango. Lentuba yayiqondana nesango lesibaya sezinkomo. Kwakwenzeka ngesinye isikhathi ukuba kube khona ezinye izintuba kulo uthango lolu, kodwa-ke izinkomo zazinga. khishwa kuzo.

  Lapho amabutho esizwe esinye ehlasela esinye isizwe, ayengathumbi kuphela izinkomo futhi ashise izindlu ngornlilo, kodwa futhi ayebulala amadoda athumbe amakhosikazi nezingane. Lezo kwakuyizinsuku zobudlova. 
  Kulezi zikhathi ezisanda kwedlula, abantu abaningi abaNsundu abafuna umsebenzi sebesondelele emadolobheni, lapho sebefice impilo yehluke kakhulu kuneyasemakhaya.   Kulezi zahluko ezilandelayo sizoke sicwaningisise amaphuzu alidlanzana empilo yabantu abaNsundu bakuqala, sihlolisise futhi nezindlela laba bantu asebaguquka ngazo.

AMAQRUGWANE 
Ezikhathini zakuqala abantu babelala emaqhugwaneni. 
Amaqhugwane lawa ayemnyama phakathi ngoba ayengenamafasitela, enomnyango owodwa kuphela, okwakuthi lapho umuntu engena ngawo agaqe ngamadolo. 
Emini wonke umuntu wayehlala phandle eshashalazini. Iqhugwane kwakulalwa kulo ebusuku, kuhlalwa kulona uma izulu lilibi, futhi kubekwa kulo izinkamba, amacansi, izikhali nokokugqoka okwakhiwe ngezikhumba, ngotshani nangobuhlalu. 
  Iphansi leqhugwane imvamisa laligandaywa ngesiduli sezintuthane, sixutshwe nobulongo negazi lenkabi. Ingaphezulu lephansi elenziwe kahle lalincwala licwebezela. 
Ingapbakatlti Iqbugwsne elinez:indonga. 
Phakathi naphakathi lapha endlini kwakukhona iziko. 
Kwakuthi uma kubasiwe intuthu ithi Iwanke, abaphakathi bakhwehlele bekhwehlelile. Kodwa-ke eningi intuthu yayifinineka ngezintutshana phakathi kwezintungo notshani iphumele ngaphandle. Phela kwakuthiwa intuthu isiza ekuxosheni ubuvunyal 
  Ngakwelinye icala kwakukhona urngibe wokubeka kahle amacansi emini lapho engasetshenziswa.

  Njengoba uthayela, uzinki, wona uyagwala, iasbhestos (engagwali njalo) ivamise ukusetshenziswa esikhundleni sikathayela. Into embi nje ukuthi iasbhestos ithanda ukwephuka masinyane. Uphahla oselwaziswa kakhulu kulezi zinsuku zanamhlanje ngolufulelwa ngothayelana abakhiwa ngezitinyana zodongwe ezishisiwe. Lokhu kubizwa futhi ngokuthi ngamasleyithi. 
  Amafasitela ezingilazi ayakhiwa ngaphandle ngakuvulande, lapho kwakuhlala khona umndeni ntambama noma ekuseni. 
  Ekuqaleni izindonga zazakhiwa ngamasoyi, kwathi kamuva kwakhiwa ngamatshe, kwase kwakhiwa ngezitini ezishisiwe-ke. Uma kwakhiwa ngezitini ezishisiwe indlu yayakhelwa emfayindishini efakwe ukhonkolo. Ukhonkolo yinhlanganisela yesihlabathi, kasimende, yohwelelezana lwamatshe namanzi. Ukhonkolo 10 uqiniswa ngokuba kufakwe izinduku zezinsimbi kuwo. Lapho lenhlanganisela isiqinile ilukhuni sadwala, kwesinye isikhathi futhi ibe lukhuni iledlule kwadwala lelo. 
  Namhlanje kukhona izindlu ezakhiwa (izindonga, iphansi nophahla) ngokhonkolo . 
  Ngesikhathi abantu behlala emaqhugwaneni nakolondo, babengenazo izindlu zokuphekela, zokugezela nezincane. Babegezela emifuleni, uma beya ngaphandle baye entabeni, baphekele phandle noma eziko kulo lelo qhugwane okwakubuywe kulalwe kulo.

khona indlu yokuphekela ngaphansi kwegosana elalixhunyelelwe odongeni ngemuva. lzimpahla zokusebenz:a erlnhlobonhJobo . 

  Kusobala ukuthi lezi zinto eziningi ezehlukile, ezenziwa ngensimbi, sezenze impilo yabalula futhi yaqokothiseka. Sekwenzeka umsebenzi omningi nongcono ngalezi zimpahla kunokuba okhokho bethu babewenza bengenazo. Mkhulu umhlabathi osulinywa ngesikhathi esincane ngamageja adonswa ngogandaganda kunalowo owawulillywa kusasetshenziswa amakhuba emikhono. Kwenzeka ifenisha eningi nenhle ngemishini esahayo Ilebazayo nelolongayo, kunokuba kusetshenziswa amazembe nemimese. Izibhamu nomagazini yizikhali zempi ezingcono kakhulu kunemikhonto nezagile. Imishini yokushicilela ikwazi ukubhala izinkulungwane zamaphephandaba akwazi ukusakaza izindaba kulo lonke izwe ngokushesha okukhulu kunalapho kusathunywa abantu bahambise imibiko, noma kumenyezwe emagqumeni. Izitimela nezimoto nezindizamshini kusiza abantu ukuba bahambe amabanga amakhulu, ngokushesha nangentokozo, kunokuba kwakunjalo ezikhathini zakudala ngaphambi kokuba lezi zinto zibe khona.

       ISAHLUKO 7 UKUDLA NENHLABATHI 

  Yilokhu kwasukela kudala abantu ukudla bakuthola emhlabathini. Ekuqaleni lokhu kwakungamabheri nezinye izithelo, izimpande ezinkulu, yiziqu ezimnandi nezinhlobo zamacembe. 

  Abantu base bebuye befunda-ke ukuthi uma befaka imbewu emhlabathini, kwakumila izithombo lapho, zigcine s~~ikhulile ~ezikhipha imbewu efanayo neyakuqala, n~ma ISlthelo eSlfanayo, amacembe afan~yo, izimpande ~Zl!anayo. Ngakho-ke base betshala Imbewu yonke U?myaka, bavuna !>adla ababekuvunile. Ezinye zalezi zltshalo kwakungezlfana namathanga, notamatisi, namapentshisi, namawolintshi; ezinye kwakungezithela noma ezihlanza phansi emhlabathini njengobhatata, namazambane; ezinye-ke zazidliwa iziqu njengemfe; nezazidliwa amacembe njengesipinashi. 

  Endulo umhlabathi wawulinywa ngabesifazane ngamakhuba emikhono. Imbewu-ke yayisakazelwa kulomhlabathi osulinyiwe, abantu bese bethandazela imvula. 

  Emva kwemvuJa, imbewu yayiqhuma, kumile izithombo ezincane. Kodwa-ke lapho kwakuthathe kukhule futhi ukhula luzoncintela izithombo ngamanzi nokudla. Yingakho nje kwakudingeka ukuba abesifazane babuye bathathe amakhuba abo bahlakule, njengoba-ke imbewu yayisakazwa nje, izithombo zazizimilela nje ngendlela yaw nangokungafani. Kwakuthi-ke lapho amakhosikazi ehlakula, agence futhi nezithombo eziningi ngenxa yokuthi kwakukade kutshalwe kwaxhotshaniselwa. Ngalendlela kwakuchithakala ngendlela engafanele ukudla okudingekayo emasimini .

  Kwathi kamuva abeLungu baletha izinhlobo eziningi zezimpahla zokulima ezase ziwusheshisa umsebenzi kakhulu.

ISAHLUKO 8 
UKUDLA (Kuyaqhutshekwa) 
IZINHLOBO ZEZILIMO EZISANHLAMYU 
  Endulo izinhlobo zezilimo ezazitshalwa ngaBantu zazingeziningi kakhulu. Kusobala ukuthi babetshala ummbila, amabele, amathanga, imifino notshani obuthile obude obuneziqu ezimnandi njengoswidi. 
  Njengoba-ke umhlabathi wawumkhulu, babekwazi ukuyishiya indawo uma bengasavuni lutho emasimini. Babenobisi oluningi, benenyama yenkomo, yembuzi nezinyamazane. 
Kodwa ngokuba umhlabathi unciphe, nezilwane zibe

114. 
yingcosana futhi zonde, nokwanda kwabantu kakhulu, kwaya kwaya yakhula inkinga yokuthola ukudla okwaneIe. Lezi zinto ezazenzeka kazenzekanga lapha eSouth Africa kuphela, kodwa nakwamanye amazwe amaningi. 
  Inkinga kwakungesikho kuphela ukuthola ukudla okwanele, kodwa kwakuyikuthola ukudla okwehlukahlukene. Odokotela basitshela ukuthi imizimba yethu idinga izinhlobo ezahlukene zokudla ukuze umuntu abe nempilo enhle. Ezinye izinhlobo zokudla (njengommbila, ngamazambane) zisinika amandla. Amandla-ke siyawadinga uma kukhona esifuna ukukwenza; okunye ukudla (njengenyama, ngobisi, ngamaqanda) kwakha imizimba yethu, bese kusiza futhi ekuhlumeleliseni inyama entsha namathambo; kanti okunye ukudla (njengemifino, nezithelo ezintsha) kusisiza ekuvikeleni izifo ezithile, nangezinye izindlela futhi. 
  Ngakho abalimi namhlanje batshala izinhlobo eziningi zezilimo. Lezi ezilandelayo ngezinye zazo: 
  I zilimo ezisanhlamvu-ummbila, ukolweni, ubhali. ioats, irayi, amabele. 
  Izilimo ezithelela ngaphansi komhlabathi-amazambane, ubhatata, amatheniphu nozanqanti, nokunye. 
  I zilimo eziluhlaza-isipinashi, iklabishi, amapentshisi, amagilebhisi, uphayinaphu, amantongomane, izindlubu, izindumba nokunye okufana nalokhu kanye notamatisi. 
IMAKETHE 
  Lapho umlimi esezivunile)zilimo zakhe uyaye azame ukuzithengisa. Uzipakisha kahle emabhokisini noma emasakeni abhalwe igama nekheli lakhe, bese ezithumela emakethe ngezinqola ngeloli noma ngesitimela. 
  Uma umlimi efuna imikhiqizo yakhe ithengise emazweni aphesheya, uyithumela ethekwini lezimpahla olwandle, lapho ifike ilayishelwe khona emkhunjini, osuzoyithatha ifike ilayishelwe khona emkhunjini, osuzoyithatha lemikhiqizo uyise eBritain noma e-Europe noma eAmerica nomaphi nje-ke futhi. 
  Imikhiqizo ibe isithengisa-ke emakethe (South Africa nakwenye indawo), bese kuthunyelwa isheke kumlimi emva kokuba sekuthathwe izindleko zemakethe. 
142 
USHINTSHO LWEMALI 
  Uma izimpahla zithunyelwa ezweni elisebenzisa imali ehlukile kulena yethu, uhlobo lwemali olukuleyo ndawo kufanele lushintshwe nohlobo lwethu. Lokhu kumelwe kwenziwe ngoba imali yakwelinye ilizwe ayinakusetshenziswa ezweni lakithi, kanjalo nemali yethu kayinakusetshenziswa kwelinye ilizwe. 
  Akesilinganise ngalokhu nje, imali esetshenziswa eUnited States of America ibizwa ngokuthiwa ngamadollars, kanti eyethu ibizwa ngokuthiwa ngamarand. Manje-ke, namhlanje irand ingangedollar nohafu. Ngakho uma umlimi eSouth Africa ethengisa imikhiqizo yakhe eUnited States of America ngamadollar alikhulu namashumi amahlanu, lemali angakhokhelwa yona eSouth Africa isilikhulu lamarand. 
UKUGCINA IMPAHLA 
  Imvamisa umlimi akazithengisi zonke izitshalo zakhe, kodwa kukhona ingxenye ayigcinayo. Angazigcina ukuze aphe izilwane zakhe azifuyile; noma angazigcina. ngob~ intengo yazo isephansi, ethemba ukuthi emva kweslkhathi intengo izokhuphuka ngonyaka olandelayo. 
  Kodwa-ke umlimi akakwazi ukuzishiya ensimini izitshalo zakhe, ngoba lapho zingabola noma zebiwe. Uyakuqoqa lokho akuvunile, bese ekugcina ezindlini zokugcina ukudla noma. impahla. Njengaleyo nd~da esizwa ngayo eBhayibhelini, wakha ingobo ukuba agcme izimpahla. 
  Uma inlpahla kuluhlobo olusheshe lonakale lubole noma izulu likahle nje (njengama-apula, ngamawolintshi, ngamazambane, ngamaqanda, ngenyama) umlimi uyigcina endaweni ebandayo enezimfanelo zakhona eqandis~ amanzi abe yiqhwa. Lendawo, enomshini wayo opholisayo, ibizwa ngokuthi yisiqandisisi. Iningi lamagciwane abanga ukubola abulawa ukubanda, kungabe kusabola-ke ukudla lokhu.

    ISAHLUKO 9 UKUFUYA IZILWANE 
  Kusukela ezikhathini ezindala aBantu bafuya izinkomo, futhi-ke bazazisa kakhulu. Endulo ubunumzane bomuntu nokunotha kwakhe kwakubonwa ngenani lezinkomo ayenazo. Imali yinto nje-ke eyayingaziwa. 
  Lapho inkosi ihola impi yayo iphuma iyohlasela ezizweni, yayethemba ukufike inqobe phambili maqedane ithumbe izinkomo. 
  Ngaphambi kokuba umuntu aganwe yintombi kwakufanele akhiphe ilobolo lalezo zinkomo abazozibiza. Inani elalejwayelekile laliba yishumi lezinkomo. Kodwa-ke indodakazi yenkosi yayilotsholwa ngamashumi amabili noma amathathu, noma futhi kweve nalapho. 
  UMzulu noma uMxhosa, noma ezinye izinhIobo zabantu abaNsundu, akukho ababekuthanda okwedlula ukubona izinkomo zeluka emagqumeni eduze nemizi. Uma umnumzane ebuka ezakhe, zazimenza azizwe enothile futhi eyindoda ebalulekile. Uma kungezesizwe, wayezizwa eziqhenya ukuthi ungaphansi kwenkosi yaleso sizwe. 
  Eqinisweni izizathu zothando olungaka lwezinkomo kuBantu kalwaziwa ukuthi luthathwaphi. ABantu babehIuleka nokuyichaza intokozo ababeyithola lapho bebona izinkomo zeluke emathafeni, zehIa zenyuka. 
144 
  Yebo, ezinye zezizathu ezenza aBantu bazikhonze kangaka izinkomo ukuthi: 
1. Izinkomo zikhipha ubisi. Ubisi-ke liwukudla okuhle kakhulu. Ubisi lolu lwethiwa eguleni bese luyekwa luvuthwa. Amnandi kanjani pho amasi egula? 
2. Inyama yenkomo lapho yosiwe imnandi kakhulu futhi yakha umzimba uqine, uphile. 
3. Izikhumba zezinkomo zisetshenziswa ekwakheni okokugqoka (izikhethi-izidwaba-zamakhosikazi, amabheshu nezinene-okwamadoda) nezikhali njengamahawu (okulwa empini noma okusina nokungcweka). 
4. Izinkomo zazidonsa izihlibhi zezinkuni. Abantu babelayisha ezihlibhini izinto abafuna ukuzithutha zisuke kwenye indawo ziye kwenye. Kwathi lapho sekusetshenziswa amageja, kwaba yizinkomo ezi. wadonsayo lapho elima, ngakho akwabe kusalinywa ngemikhono. 
  Kwaba kubi nje-ke kodwa ngoba kwathi noma ngokuhamba kwesikhathi, umhIabathi usuncipha, omusha ungasatholakali, aBantu kabaze bazama ukunciphisa izinkomo zabo zilingane nendawo leyo eyase ikhona. Babesafuna izinkomo zande, ngisho utshani babungasezukuzenela. Izinkomo zabo-ke zagcina sezondile futhi sezizincane. 
  Ziningi izinkomo ezafa ngenxa yalokhu; kodwa nokho kwaba khona ezinye ezazizala zanda, kodwa utshani bona baya njalo ngokuncipha. Kwafika umoya nemvula wasusa ugqimba lomhIabathi ongaphezulu, kwathi izingxenye eziningi eSouth Africa zaguguleka umhlabathi ngendlela eyaba yingozi. 
  ABantu futhi babefuye ezinye izilwane, njengezimvu nezimbuzi, ukuze bathole inyama nezikhumba. 
  Kodwa-ke kwabuye kwaphinda sona leso futhi kulezi zilwane esenzeka ezinkomeni; zadedelwa zanda kakhulu kazabe zisayenela indawo eyayikhona. Umphumela wukuthi izilwane lezi kazibanga zinhIe, zondleke, kanti-ke namanani azo amakhulu akuqhubela phambili ukuguguleka komhIabathi.

  Sekuyisikhathi eside uHulumeni ezama ukufundise aBantu izinto ezisemqoka ngemfuyo. 
(a) Uzama ukubagqugquzela ukuba bayinciphise imfuyo yabo ukuze kube khona utshani obanele leyo naleyo nkomo. 
(b) Uzama ukubafundisa amasu okuba nohlobo oluhle lwemfuyo, ngokuba kusetshenziswe izinkunzi nezimpongo zohlobo. UHulumeni wathumela walanda nohlobo lwemvu okuthiwa yiMerino, enovolo omningi omuhle. Ngokuzalanisa uhlobo IweMerino nohlobo olwalukhona kulelizwe kuqala, kwavela uhlobo oluhle Iwezimvu olwaba novolo omuhle. 
(c) UHulumeni uyazama futhi ukugqugquzela aBantu ukuba imfuyo yabo bayitshalele ukudla kokuyihlinzeka ebusika ngesikhathi utshani bomile. 
  Labo Bantu abenza lokhu ibathokozisa kakhulu imiphumela. Izinkomo zabo seziyingcosana kunalokho ezaziyikhona, kodwa kutholakala kuzo ubisi oluningi. Kwezinye izifunda aBantu sebahlangana benza amaCooperative Societies, athenga ubisi nokhilimu kubakhiqizi balezi zinto, enze ibhotela noshizi, bese ethengisa ubisi, ukhilimu, ibhotela noshizi kulabo bantu abahlala emadolobheni. 
Izinkabi ziyingcosana kodwa zinkulu futhi zinamandla. 
Zikwazi ukwenza umsebenzi omningi; kanti futhi amasilaha athengisa inyama azithenga ngemali enkulu. Futhi iningi inyama yemvu ekhiqizwa yizimvu eziyingcosane. Kanjalo novolo wezimvu eziyingcosane mningi. 
  Okunye futhi: Izikhumba zalezi zinkomo nezimvu zishukwa emafektri okushuka izikhumba zibe yizikhumba ezingcono kunezikhumba zezilwane ezondile, ezingondlekile nakahle. Izikhumba ezinhle zithengwa ngemali enhle kakhulu. 
  Omunye umphumela omuhle ukuthi ukuguguleka komhlabathi kulezo zindawo sekunqotshiwe, notshani osebumile emhlabathini sebu buningi. 
  Ezikhathini ezedlule kwakusetshenziswa izinkabi ekudonseni amafulaha, athwelwe yizihlibhi nezinqola. Namageja ayedonswa yizo izinkabi. ABantu nabeLungu

UMSEBENZI OHAN]ELWAYO 

  Njengoba sesibonile, aBantu abaningi besilisa nesifazane bashiya amakhaya abo emaphandleni noma ezabelweni bayofuna umsebenzi emadolobheni. 

  Uma behluleka ukuthola umsebenzi edolobheni elilodwa, bayaharnba baye kwelinye idolobha. Basuka kanjena-ke edolobheni elilodwa baye kwelinye. 

  Amadolobha akakwazi ukuba nomsebenzi wabo bonke abantu, kanti futhi awanazo izindlu ezenele lapho abantu bengahlala khona. Ngenxa yalokhu-ke arnadolobh~ kawavumi ukuba bangene bonke aBantu emadolobhem. UHulumeni sewenza imithetho mayelana nalokhu. Kuwo wonke amadolobha kukhona izikhulu eziqikelela ukuba lemithetho igcinwe. Omunye umthetho yilona othi urnuntu okufanele abe sedolobheni yilowo oqhashwe lapho kuphela. 

  Abanye aBantu, njengoba sesizwil~, ba~a~arnba bay~sebenza kurnaEstates kashukela, eZlmayml, emafektn; kuthi uma sebeshiya imisebenzi yabo noma besayophumula kancane, baqonde emakhaya ezabelweni nasemaphandleni. 

  Izinkulungwane zezisebenzi zaBantu zihlala njalo zihamba zisuka edolobheni elilodwa ziqonde kwelinye, zisuke kulomsebenzi ziye komunye, noma zisuke edolobheni, emayini noma efektri ziphindele emakhaya futhi.

  Kulemifanekiso elandelayo uzobona inqubekela phambili eyaba khona.

   ISAHLUKO 12 AMASIKO KAZULU 

UKWESHWAMA: Leli isiko lokubonga ukudla emasimini Ilokuqinisa isizwe. Kwakweshwama inkosi emzini wayo abantu babuthane khona. Ukudla okusha emasimini kwakungadliwa lingakenziwa lelisiko. Lapho-ke iN kosi isilenzile ishwamo, abantu babeqala ukuwudla immbila omusha nokunye, kuthi lapho bewudla bathi: "Dolo qinal Dolo qina'" 

UNOMKHUBULWANA: Kwakunenkolo yokuthi uNomkhubulwana yiNkosazana yezulu. Nguye owayepha abantu inala. UNomkhubulwana wayenensimu yakhe. Yayilinywa ngamakhosikazi wonke esigodi, itshalwe. Lensimu yayingahlakulwa futhi yayingavunwa. 

ILOBOLO: Yizinkomo ezikhishwa ngabakubo kamkhwenyana zinikwe abakubo ntombi ezogana. Kuqala umuntu wayekhipha lokho anakho, kungekho sibalo esimisiwe. Namuhla ilobolo ishumi lezinkomo nenkomo eyodwa. Abanumzane, nezinduna namakhosi bona balotsholelwa ngezinkomo ezingaphezulu kwalokho. Esikhathini samanje sekwanda ukulobola ngemali kanti sekukhona nabangalobolisi. . 

UKUCIMELA: Uma intombazane isizogana ihambela izihlobo iyovalelisa. Izihlobo-ke ziyipha izipho eziningi. Lokhu kuvalelisa nokuphiwa izipho kubizwa ngokuthi ukucimela. 

UKWEMULA: Kwemuliswa intombazane. Yemuliswa nguyise uma isikhulile isifanele ukugana. Uyihlabela inkomo enze idili. Kuyadliwa kusinwe kujatshulwe. Emva kokwenziwa kwalelisiko intombazana isingagana. UKWABA: Uma umakoti egana uza nezipho azozipha abasemzini lapho eganela khona. Lokhu-ke kubizwa ngokuthi wukwaba noma ukugezisa. Kuqala umakoti wabe aba ngamacansi, ngemishanelo, ngamahluzo nokunye. Namuhla sekukhona ababa ngempahla yokuthengwa, amaragi, imiqamelo, njalonjalo .

UKUBULALA IGULA: Yisiko elenziwa lapho izihlobo ziganene zingazi. Inkolo wukuthi uma lingenziwanga lelisiko bayozala abantwana abayizilima. Kuhlatshwa imbuzi emhlophe. 
UKUGWEBA IZINGANE: Lokhu kusho ukuphehla ingane ngemuva kukhishwe igazi elibizwa ngokuthi igazi elibi. Kuphehlwa ngoluthi. Kuphehlwa abantwana abaseminyakeni elishumi. Inkolo kwabe kuwukuthi uma ingane ingaphehlwanga ikhula nemikhuba emibi, ingabi nesimilo esihle. 
UKUKLEKLA NOMA UKUQHUMBUZA: Leli isiko lokubhoboza izindlebe. Kukleklwa abantwana babafana nabamantombazana. Kwenziwa lapho beseyizithohlongwana nje. Ukuqhumbuza esikhathini esiphambili kwakwenziwa ezinganeni ezintanganye sonke isigodi. Namuhla abantu abaningi abasaligcini lelisiko. 
ISAHLUKO 13 
IZIFIKI ZOKUQALA ECAPE 
  Akusibo aBantu noma abeLungu abafika kuqala eSouth Africa. Iminyaka engamakhulu ngaphambi kokuba zombili lezi zizwe zifike lapha, kwase kufike isizwe esinemizinjana emincane okwathi ernuva kwesikhathi sathola igama, kwathiwa ngabaThwa. Lesi sizwe sasihlala ezingxenyeni eziningi kulelizwe. 
  Kodwa nangaphambi kwabo abaThwa laba, kwakukhona abantu eSouth Africa asebebizwa ngokuthiwa manje ngamaBoskop noma ngamaStra1ldlojJers. 
AMASTRANDLOPERS 
  Kuncane kabi esikwaziyo ngamaStrandlopers. Laba bantu babakha izimpahla zokusebenza ngamatshe, kodwa izimpahla zabo zehlukile kulezo ezazenziwa ngabaThwa; kanti-ke nophahla Iwemizimba yabo lukhombisa ngokusobala ukuthi babeyisizwe esehlukile kubaThwa. 
  Uphahla Iwemizimba yabo, kanye nenye ingxenye yezimpahla zokusehenza namabhodwe, ababekwenza,

kutholakala eduze kolwandle. Ngakho-ke sicabanga ukuthi laba bantu babehlala ngasoGwini. Kodwa-ke kungenzeka futhi ukuthi babehlalela phakathi nalo izwe, ayi kuphela oGwini.

nyoka, izintethe, izibankwa, konke lokhu abaThwa babekudla uma bekubambile noma bekucibe l1gemicibisholo kwafa. 

  Babedla futhi izirnpande, arnacembe nezithelo zezihlahla eziningi. Lolu hlobo lokudla-ke lwaluqoqwa ngamakhosikazi namantombazane. 

  AbaThwa babengalimi mhlabathi bengatshali mbewu bengafuye nkomo, yirnvu nambuzi. 

  AbaThwa babengahlukene njengabantu abaNsundu ababehlezi ngezizwana ezehlukene. AbaThwa babehlala ngamaqoqwana alindele ukuzingela. Ubuningi balamaqoqo babuba ngamashumi amahlanu noma ikhulu namashumi amahlanu. Kwakuyilelo nalelo qoqwana lokuzingela lizihlalele buqamu nelinye futhi libe nenduna noma nenkosi yalo. 

  Njengoba-ke abaThwa, njengabo bonke abantu nje, bewadinga amanzi, babevamise ukwakha amaxhokovanyana abo ngamahlamvu ababehlala kuwona eduze kwemifula. Babelala kuwona futhi amaxhokovana lawa. 

  Uma behlale lapho kungekho mifula khona, babefuna imithombo yamanzi, bese bemisa arnaxhokovanyana abo-ke eduze nje nakulezo zindawo okutholakale kuzo amanzi. 

  Vma imithombo lena isha, iqoqwana labantu lelo lalithutha liyomisa arnaxhokovana eduze nalapho kwakutholakale arnanzi kabusha. Uma njalo begcine bengawatholanga arnanzi, kwakuze kubabulale nje nya ukoma bangcwatshwe impela. 

  Abanye abaThwa, babehlala emigedeni emagqumeni nasezintabeni. Lapha ezindongeni zarnatshe zalemigede, 

abadwebi babaThwa babedweba izilwane, abantu bezingela noma belwa. AbaThwa lokhu babekudweba ngemibala etholakala ezinhlotsheni ezahlukene zenhlabathi, zamadwala nezitshalo. Norna lemidwebo yadwetshwa iminyaka engamakhulu eyadlula, imibala lena isakhanya ngendlela ecace ngokumangalisayo. 

  Ezinye izazi zemifanekiso zabaThwa zazingasebenzisi irnibala, kodwa imifanekiso yezilwane nabantu zaziyenza ngokuqopha ematsheni. 

  Kukholwa ukuthi ikhaya lokuqala labaThwa liseCentral Africa, nokuthi makube basuswa lapho ngabantu abanamandla kakhulu kunabo. 
AMALAWU 
AmaLawu afika eSouth Africa kamuva kunabaThwa. 

Nawo amaLawu kucatshangwa ukuthi ayephuma phakathi nayo iAfrica. Bona-ke laba bantu babethe ukuba bade kancane kodwa isikhumba sabo sasingumbala of ana yo nobuso babo bufana. 

  Nabo babegqoka izikhumba zezilwane. Kodwa-ke bona babefike behluke kubaThwa ngoba bona babewahlobisa arnabheshu abo, futhi benza nezipheqwana zokwembatha emahlombe, kanye nokokubeka okhalweni.

  Amaqoqo amaningi ezizwana ngezizwana ayeyizihlobo ayehamba ndawonye, noma alandelane eduze. Yingakho nje kwathi lapho sezifika eNingizimu Africa izizwe eziNsundu, zafika zingamadlanzi amakhulu kugcwele abantu abazalanayo. 
  Sithola ukuthi-ke iqembu elikhulu labantu abaNsundu, elaziwa ngokuthi ngamaOvambo-Herero, lafika kanyekanye (noma lalandelana eduze). Ngaphambi kokuba bawele Umfula iZambesi, baphendukela ngasentshonalanga ezweni elibizwa ngokuthi yiSouth West Africa. 
  Elinye iqembu elikhulu futhi labantu abaNsundu kwakuyizizwe zabeSuthu nabeTswana. AbeTswana bona bazinza eBotswana. AbeSuthu bakha Imlzl yabo ezweni elibizwa ngokuthi yiWestern Transvaal, eFree State naseLesotho. 
  Iqembu elikhulu labahlaseli kwakungelabaNguni. Leli iqembu elagcina selibe ngamaXhosa namaZulu. Kodwake kulelo qembu kwakukhona futhi okhokho bezizwe ezaziwa namhlanje ngokuthi ngabaThembu, ngamaFingo, ngamaMpondo nabanye. 
  Leli qembu lesithathu elikhulu lalihamba ngezigaba liqonde ezansi empumalanga yeSouth Africa phakathi kwezintaba nolwandle. 
  AbaThembu namaXhosa bahamba baqhubeka baqonda eningizimu base bakha eduze kweMifula iFish neKei. AmaFingo namaMpondo wona aba ngasenyakatho yabaThembu namaXhosa. Emva kwesikhathi eside lezi zizwe ezahlukene zangaseningizimu zamaNguni zazinza ezweni elaziwa ngokuthi namhlanje yiTranskei. 
  Ekuqaleni amaZulu ayeyisizwe esincane, ehlala ezweni eliphakathi kweMifula iBlack neWhite Umfolozi. Kodwa-ke kungakapheli sikhathi eside, ngesikhathi sokubusa kukaShaka, amaZulu anqoba lonke elaseZululand nelaseNatal. 
  Kuyasikhanyela-ke ukuthi kwaba khona ukufuduka okukhulu kwabantu abaNsundu beqonde eningizimu. Siyakubona futhi ukuthi izizwe ezahlukene zabaNsundu zazinza ngamaqoqwana ayeyizihlobo ezindaweni ezehlukene zaseSouth Africa.

  Leligama elithi "Turks" lapha liqonde izlzwe eziningi zase Asia Minor, Syria, Palestine, Arabia Egypt. 

  Ngenkolo babekholwe kuMohammed. Iminyaka eminingi amakholwa kaMohammed kanye namakholwa kaKristu ayelokbu elwa. Manje abakaMohammed baphumelela ukuvalela abeLungu base-Europe ukuba badabule kulamazwe. 

  Kanjalo-ke eminyakeni engamakhulu amahlanu eyedlulayo yavalwa imigudu emidala yohwebo phakathi kwe-Europe neAsia.

IZINKAMBO NGOLWANDLE NOKUTHOLWA KWENDAWO 
UDIAZ NODAGAMA 

  Nakuba imigudu leyo emidaladala yohwebo ebange empumalanga yayisivalekile abeLungu lena e-Europe babelokhu bezidingile izimpahla zaseChina, naseIndia, nasePersia nakwamanye amazwe asempumalanga. 

  Bafunisisa bacabangisisa ukuthi bangafinyelela yini ngendlela ehlahlela olwandle engezukubayisa emazweni anabalandeli bakaMohammed. 

  Phela ngalesisikhathi abeLungu babazi inxenyana encane nje yomhlaba. Lenxenyana eyayaziwa kwabe kuyileyo yase-Europe nenxenye yaseAsia kanye neyaseAfrica enhIa nalo. 

  Abantu lena e-Europe babengazi ukuthi izwe laseAfrica liphelelaphi eningizimu. Baqala ukucabanga ukuthi konje kungenzeka yini ukuba imikhumbi ikwazi ukuhamba izungeze iAfrica ize iyofika elndia ngolwandle.

Ngalokho wayekhombisa ukuthi useze wayofika kuleyondawo okwakungakaze kufike muntu kuyo ehamba ngogu IwaseAfrica. Ngaso leso siphambano futhi wayekhombisa ukubonga kuM velingqangi. 
  Esuka lapho wahamba epheshethwakahleumoya cishu amasonto amabili. Waguquka umoya kwaqhamuka isivunguvungu esinamandla esayithatha imikhunjana lena yaye 

yedlula lapho iAfrica iphelela khona eningizimu. Lapho uDiaz wabe esathalaze phinde alibone izwe, futhi wayengazi ukuthi usedlule isinqe seAfrica. Ukuze athole kahle indlela yakhe waphendula imikhunjana yakhe wahamba waqonda enyakatho, wathi ethuka wayesebona izwe, indawo esiyibiza namuhla ngokuthi yiMossel Bay. Wafika wakhumula lapho waphinda futhi wagxumeka isiphambano enhlabathini lapho. 

  Kwathi uma esecabangisisa wabona ukuthi usesedlule impela isinqe seAfrica kodwa ukuze abenalo iqiniso eliphelele wahamba waqonda empumalanga egudla lona njalo ugu lolwandle. Wafumanisa ukuthi seluqonda enyakatho-mpumalanga. Wabona ngempela ukuthi uselizungezile iAfrica, waqiniseka ukuthi nakanjani uma engahamba njalo aqhubeke usengaye afike elndia. 

  Kepha omatilosi base bekhathele, abanye sebegula, futhi nomphako wabo usuphelile. Nempela waphendula imikhumbi yakhe ehamba ephindela emuva eyokwedlula eCape, waqombothisa wabanga kwelakubo ePortugal ebaphathele izindaba ezinkulu.

              ISAHLUKO 17 IZINKAMPANI EZINKULU ZASEINDIA 
  Izwe lasePortugaI kwakungesilona lodwa elalinamatilosi ahlakaniphile futhi anesibindi. Amazwe aseHolland nase-England naseFrance nawo ayenemikhumbi emini. ngi namadoda ayizindela ayezidelile ukuba ahambe lapha kulezizilwandlekazi. Kulesisahluko sizozwa ngeHolland ne-England. 
1 mUTCH EAST INDIA COMPANY 
  Abantu baseHolland nabo futhi. basukuma phansi bathumela imikhumbi khona kweliphesheya ukuba iyohweba. Emva kwesikhathi baqala ukuhweba neIndia neChina neziqhingana eziseduze nalezo zindawo. 
  Elwandle lapha imikhumbi lena yamaPortuguese yayilwa njalo nalena yamaHolland ngoba ingathandi ukuba amaHollandi nawo asebenzelane namazwe asempumalanga. Kodwa emva kwesikhathi amaHollandi awuthatha wonke lomsebenzi. amaPortuguese ehluleka. 
  Kusasuka phansi imikhumbi yamaHollandi kwabe kungeyezinkampani ezincane. Zaziholela amatilosi lezizinkampani zona zithathe inzuzo evezwa yilowo msebenzi wohwebo. 
  Kepha lemikhumbi yayiyingcosana. Ngakho-ke yayehlulwa kalula yizitha ziyiphange noma ziyicwilise. Ngalokho-ke lezi zinkambo zohwebo elwandle zabe zinengozi kakhulu. Ngakho-ke ngomyaka ka-1602 lezizinkampani ezincane zahlangana zakha inkampani enkulu eyayinamandla kakhulu kunezitha zayo. Lenkampani enkulu yathumela imikhumbi eminingi ngasikhathi sinye futhi yakwazi ukuyihlomisa kahle . 
 . Ngoba lamazwe lenkampani eyayithengiselana nawo i-India neI3urrna, neMaIaya neSumatra, neBorneo, neJava namanye ayebizwa ngokuthi yiEast Indies, lenka- 
177 




142. 
mpani enkulu entsha yabizwa ngokuthi yiDutch East India Company. 
  UHulumeni waseHolland wavuma ukuba lenkampani enkulu yakhiwe, kwase kumiswa umgwamanda wamadoda alishumi nesikhombisa ukuba ayiphathe. LeNkampani yayinikwe onke amandla, hayi mayelana nohwebo nje kuphela, kodwa ngisho nokuhlaselisa impi nokwakha amathanga kwamanye amazwe futhi ibeke ababusi bokubusa kulawo mathanga amasha. 
  Nempela lamandla iNkampani yawasebenzisa, yakha umbuso omkhulu wohwebo empumalanga. Yakha amafektri nezinqaba, nezindawo zohwebo. Lezizindawo kuhambe kwahamba zaba amadolobha amakhulu. 
  Esiqhingini saseJava iNkampani yakha idolobha elikhulu elibizwa ngokuthi Batavia okuyilona elaba yikomkhulu yalombuso wohwebo kwelaseMpumalanga. Lapho-ke eBatavia kwakhethwa umgwamanda wamadoda ukuba abuse abheke konke abhekele umgwamanda omkhulu ophesheya wamadoda alishumi nesikhombisa. 
  Ukumiswa kweDutch East India Company nokwakhiwa kwalombuso wohwebo kwaba nomphumela lapha eSouth Africa njengoba sizobona. 
2 IENGLISH EAST INDIA COMPANY Njengoba kwenza amaPutukezi namaHollandi nawo amaNgisi anyakaza aphokophela yon a intengo nentengiso khona eEast Indies. 
  Njengawo amaHollandi nawo aqala ngezinkampani ezincane kodwa abona ukuthi ukuze akwazi ukulwa nezitha azihlangane lezizinkampani zakhe eyodwa inkampani enamandla; nempela amisa inkampani enkulu, iEnglish East India Company. 
  LeNkampani yamaNgisi yona yamiswa ngomnyaka ka-l,600 ngosuku lokugcina ngci lomnyaka lowo. Kwacisho kwedlula isikhathi esingaphezulwana konyaka imisiwe leNkampani ngaphambi kokuba kumiswe IDutch East India Company. 
  Kwabekukhona umbango nokuphikisana okukhulu phakathi kwalezizinkampani ezimbili ezinkulu. Ngesinye isikhathi bekuliwa zitholane phezulu kuthule ozaqi 
178 
kuthi ngoba nakhu amandla ayalingana kungaze kwehlulwa muntu. 
  Isigcino lezizinkampani zavumelana ukuba kwahlukaniselwane izindawo lapha kwelaseMpumalanga yikhona kuzosetshenzwa kahle. AmaNgisi avuma ukuba anqandele asebenze eIndia namazwe ahlangene nayo, namaHollandi anqandela wona asebenza eziq hingini ezibizwa ngokuthi Dutch East Indies, nasemazweni aphambili nempumalanga iChina neJapan. 
  Naye uHulumeni wamaNgisi inkampani lena wayigidlabeza ngamandla amakhulu abanzi anjengawo lawo anikezwa iDutch East India Company nguHulumeni waseHollandi. Kwaqhubeka isikhathi inkampani yamaNgisi yaceha kakhulu kangangokuba yaba numandla amakhulu kwelase-India. Kwathi phakathi kwekhulu neshumi nesishiyagalolunye umsebenzi wayo leNkampani yase iwunikeza uHulumeni wamaNgisi.

          ISAHLUKO 18 UKUPHIHLIZEKA KWEHAARLEM 
  Ngezinsuku zeziNkampani ezinkulu zasempumalanga imikhumbi yokuthwala izimpahla yayimincane futhi yayihamba kuphela uma isunduzwa ngumoya. Ukwelekelela ukuba umoya ukwazi ukuba uyidudule kahle lemikhumbi kwakufakwa oseyili abakhulu baboshelwe ezigxotsheni ezinde. Leyo mikhumbi yayingenazo izinjini njengalemikhumbi yanamuhla. 
  Ngenxa yokuhamba ngoseyili ukusuka eHolland noma e-England uya e-East Indies kwabe kuthatha isikhathi p.side. Uhambo beluqeda izinyanga eziyisithupha noma ligaphezulu. 
  Esikhathini eside kangako bekuthi kusahanjwa ukudla ilamanzi emkhunjini kubole ngoba zazingakabikho izindlela zokuba kuhlale kubanda kungonakali. Ngalesosizathu amatilosi ayevama ukugula amanye afe endleni. 
\80 
  Kwafumaniseka ukuthi kufanela kube khona indawo ephakathi nendawo lapho kungatholakala khona izithelo, imifino nenyama namanzi. 
  Kwafinyaniseka ukuthi kufanele kubekhona abantu abakhile kuleyo ndawo ukuze balime lezizinto ezidingwa yimikhumbi edlulayo futhi nayo imikhumbi iqiniseke ukuthi izokuthola lokhu ekudingayo. 
  Imikhumbi yayide ima ikhumule ethekwini laseCape okwathi emveni kwesikhathi labizwa ngokuthi kuseTable Bay. Lapha ibifika ikhe amanzi amasha, ngesiuye isikhathi amatilosi adubule nezinyamazane. . 
  Ngelinye ilanga ngomnyaka ka-1647 imikhumbi yamaBhunu yayimi nje lapha kulelitheku isaphumule. Yayiqonde ekhaya eHolland. Kwaqhamuka isivunguvungu, iHaarlem yaphihlizeka ematsheni. Ngenhlanhla amatilosi onke aphuma engafile kanye nabanye ababekhwele kuwo. Nempahla eyakulomkhumbi yasinda. Kepha impahla yalomkhumbi yayingakwazi ukuthwalwa yilemikhumbi eminye ngoba nayo yayigcwele kakhulu. 
  Ngakho-ke kwathi uma lemikhumbi emmye isisuka ihamba ibange ekhaya eHolland induna yatshela amatilosi angamashumi ayisithupha ukuba wona asale abheke izimpahla ezikhishwe kulomkhumbi owawucwilile iHaarlem. Babezosala laba abasalayo bebhekwe wuLeenderf Jansgoon baze bathole umkhumbi ongabelekelela. 
  Lamatilosi asala lapha azakhela amadlangala azihlalela khona aphila ngezinyamazane kanye nezinhlanzi ababezidoba. Batshala futhi nemifino, pho ngoba kwakuvundile yakhula yakhephezela. 
  Bahlala kahle ngokuthula namaLawu, babona ukuthi awanalo uchuku uma kuhlalisenwe kahle ngokuthula behlonishwa ngemfanelo. 
  Kwathi ngonyaka olandelayo ngo-1648 kwafika eminye imikhumbi yenkampani eyayivela e-East Indies. Yabacosha nempahla leyo yeHaariem yahamba nabo yabanga eHolland. 
  Bathe lapho befika eHolland abaholi benza umbiko omuhle ngeCape. Bathi yindawo enempilo enhle okungatshalwa kuyo izithelo nemifino ngaphandle kokukhathazeka. Bathi amaLawu angabantu abalungile uma bephe-

UJobao Tan Riebeeck 
thwe kahle ngemfanelo futhi banam izinkomo rokuthengisa. 
  IDuteh East India Company yayiyi£Una kakhulu indawo enjalo. Ngoba nakhu umbiko wawumuhle kangaka umgwamanda wamadoda alishumi nesikhombisa wanquma ikuthumela abantu abathize ukuyotshala izingadi futhi batshale nezithel0, bathenge izinkomo kumaLaViU. 
  Ngaleyondlela amatilosi emikhumbi yeNkampani ayewba nalo iqiniso lokufica imifino nezithelo nenyama lapho. Lokhu kwabe kuzosiza ukuba ukugula nokufa emikhunjini kungandi kuvame njengoba kwabe kuvamile.

ISAHLUKO 19 
UKUFIKA KUKAJAN VAN RIEBEECK ECAPE 
  Sesifundile ukuthi amatilosi asala ngemuva ngesikhathi sokuphihlizeka kweHaariem aphila kahle elindele imikhumbi yokuwaphindisela eHolland. Sesikufundile futhi nokuthi afika abika lamatilosi ukuthi iCape indawo enhle. Lemibiko-ke yenza iDuteh East India Company ibone ukuthi iCape yiyona yona indawo lapho ifaneic imise isikhumulo semikhumbi lapho ingathola khona ukudla namanzi. Iziphathimandla zeNkampani ezabe zaziwa ngokuthi yisigungu sabayishumi nesikhombisa kwase kudingeka-ke ukuba zikhethe okunguyena ozohola labo abazoya komisa lesisikhumulo eCape. Umuntu-ke abamkhetha kwabe kunguJan van Riebeeek owabe eyisise- 
benzi sayo iNkampani. 
  U Jan van Riebeeek wasuka eHolland namadoda angamakhulu amabili. Babehamba ngemikhumbi emincane emithathu. Lolu hambo lwabathatha eisho izinyanga ezintathu. Masikhumbule ukuthi ukuhamba olwandle ngalezo zikhathi kwakunezingozi eziningi kanti £Uthi kwakungekho bumnandi emikhunjini yangalezo zikhathi. Lemikhunjana yahlangabezana nezingozi zeziphepho zasolwandle; yahlangabezana nezingozi zokuphelelwa ngumoya ngoba phela imikhumbi yabe iqhutshwa ngumoya ngalezo zikhathi; yahlangabezana nezingozi rokubheduka kwezifo komatilosi nabanye 
183 







.. _. ------------------------------------------ 
ababehamba ngemikhumbi uma ukudka namanzi sekonakala. Kwabe kukhona nengozi futhi yokuthi uma imikhumbi ima esizalweni somfula ngenhloso yokufuna amanzi, hleze ihlaselwe izizwe ezakhile lapho. Kanti kwabe kukhona nengozi yokulunywa yimiyane, omatilosi bahlaselwe wukufa koqhuqho nezinye izifo ezithwalwa yimindozolwane. Phela ngalezozinsuku yabe ingakabibikho imithi yokwelapha lezi zifo; baningi-ke omatiJosi ezabe zibabulala. 
  Kusobala-ke ukuthi naye uvan Riebeeek nayehamba nabo baeabanga ngazo zonke lezizingozi ngaphambi kokuba basuke eHoliand. Kepha noma kunjalo baphuma ngesibindi esikhulu, bahamba baze bayofinyelela eCape ngo-April, 1652. (Minyaka yonke sinosuku esikhumbula ngalo lokho kufika kuka van Riebeeek). 
  Kuthe-ke lapho efika eCape, uvan Riebeeek wawuqalisa umsebenzi. Isigungu Sabayishumi Nesikhombisa esabe simbekele won a ukuba awenze. Nazi-ke izinto abe eyalwe ukuba azenze:- 
1. Alime izivande atshale imifino anikeze imikhumbi yabo edlulayo evela elndia noma esaya khona. Ezivandeni atshale futhi nezithelo. 
2. Akhe amanzi amahle abone nokuthi ayatholakala noma ngasiphi isikhathi. 
3. Ahlalisane kahle ngokuthula namaLawu athenge izinkomo kuwo ukuze kutholakale inyama njalo yemikhumbi yabo. 
4. Akhe inqaba ukuze bazivikele ezitheni eziqhamuka elwandle noma ezweni. 
  Uvan Riebeeek nabantu bakhe bawufumanisa lomsebenzi unzima kakhulu futhi kwakuvamile nokuba kuvele izinto ezibadumazayo. 
  Iziphepho nezivunguvunguzagugula izivande zabo, nezimfene zehla ezintabeni zafohloza izilimo zathatha izithelo zemuka nazo. Kwabuya kwasuka iziphithiphithi baxabana namaLawu. Nabantu bakhe babevame ukuhlaselwa yizifo. Kepha noma kunjalo uvan Riebeeek wakwazi ukuphumelelisa lokho abe ekuthunyiwe ukuba akwenze. 
IMIBUZO 
1. Ngubani owathumela uJan van Riebeeek eCape? 
2. Wafika ngamuphi umnyaka uvan Riebeeek eCape? 
3. Kwakuthiwe makenzeni eCape uvan Riebeeek na. bantu bankhe? 
4. Lemikhumbi eyabe ingenisa esikhumulweni saseCape yabe iyaphi? 
5. Zizwe zini ezabe zihlala eCape ngaphambi kokufika kukaJan van Riebeeek?

IZIMISELO NEMISEBENZI 
  Ingane kufanele ikuzwe egazini ukuthi "Leli yilokishi lami, leli yidolobha !ami." Uma ingane ikuzwa lokhu ngokungangabazisi. iyophatheka kabi uma indawo eyazisayo neziqhenya ngayo ingahlanzekile, ingcolile, ingenampilo nabahlala khona beyimidlwempe nje kungekho mthetho abawugcinayo futhi bengenabungani. Ingane iyozama yona ngokwayo, igqugquzele nabangani bayo futhi ukuba into enjalo ingadedelwa yenzeke. 
  Kanti-ke ingane igcwala umoya wentokozo nokuziqhenya uma indawo ehlala kuyo iyinhle, inempilo. ihlanzekile, izihlali khona ziyigcina imithetho futhi zinobungani. Yenza konke okusemandleni ayo ukuba lokhu kuhlale kunje kungaphazantisekI. 
  Lokhu-ke kusho ukuthi ingane lena izizwa inezimiselo ezithile mayelana nelokishi layo. futhi izimisele ukwenza imisebenzi ethile ukuze izimiselo zayo zifezeke. 
   Lokhu okulandelayo kungokunye kwalemisebenzi: (a) Iyo7.ama ukuhlonipha yonke imithetho yelokishi • . futhi izame nokugqugquzela abangani bayo ukuba bangephuli mithetho nabo. Lemithetho. futhi uma sekubhekisiswa. kayimiswa nje ngoba kuhloswe ukujabulisa labo abaphethe. kepha yenzelwa ukuphepha nentokozo yabo bonke abantu abahlala elokishini. 
  Ukuba yayingekho imithetho evimba ukuba kubulawe impahla, okungabafana nokungamantombazane okunamakhanda angalungile kwakungahamba kubulala iminyango namafasitela ezindlu zabantu, kugidagide ezingadini zabantu, kubeke amagatsha ezihlahla emigwaqweni ukuze kuthikaziseke abezi.moto, kubulale izigxobo zikagesi emigwaqeni, kuthi ngesikhashana nje ilokishi libe libi futhi libe yingozi.

ngernpela ukuthi sinenhlanhla ukuba narnakhaya thina esingathi ngawethu. 
IZIMISELO 
  Izirniselo zezingane ekhaya zisafana nje Ilemisebenzi yazoo Sifuna ukwenezezela kodwa ngaphansi kwalesi sihloko ukuthi yilowo nalowo muntu ekhaya kufanele azizwe enezimiselo ezithile kwabomndeni wakubo. Uma kukhona owomndeni osebunzimeni, abanye bakubo akufanele bambukelele bangamsizi. Uma omunye evelelwe yingozi waJi:nala, noma egula kufanele abanye bamda~ukele bamslZe, kube khona nabakwenzayo kokumjabulisa. Uma omunye wabo eveielwa yinhlanhla ethile noma kukhona into ayenze kahle kakhulu, aballye aku~ fanele bamumonazele, kepha kufanele bathokoze naye futhi baziqhenye ngaye. Uma kukhona odukayo, ofun~ ukwenza i.<;enzo esingesihle, bonke abomndeni bazama ukumkhuza, kuthi uma behluleka, badabuke kakhulu. Nokho kodwa bahlala bemthanda Iljalo naphezu kokubadumaza kwakhe. 
  Ngalendlela-ke yilowo nalowo womndeni unezimiselo hayi. kuphela mayelana nokuziphatha kwakhe, keph~ futhi kufanele anakekele abanye. Imisebenzi yakhe uy:nza k~~ ngokunike)a, uma k.udingekile asize nabanye emISebenzmI yabo futhI, ukuze ikhaya nornndeni wonke kube nentokozo zonke izinto khona zihambe kahle.

UKUZIPHATHA KAHLE ESIKOLENI NAKUBAZALI. IMISEBENZI YENGANE. IZIMISELO 
	NAMATHUBA 	AYO 	ESIKOLENI 
IMISEBENZI NEZIMISELO 
(a) Ingane kufanele iye esikoleni njalo ingaphuthi, futhi Hike ngesikhathi. 
(b) Kufanele imhloniphe uthisha wayo futhi ilalele ukuthi uthini. 
(e) K ufanele ithule ngesikhathi kufundiswa, ingabe ilokhu ibhiyoza, ngoba umsindo uyabathikazisa abanye. (d) Kufanele umzimba wayo nezingubo zayo kuhla. nzeke. Kumele futhi ukuba yelekelele ekuhlanzweni kwezindlu okufundelwa kuzona kanye nokwamagceke. Vma ingane ibona amaphepha nenye imfucuza kufanele iwacoshe iwafake emgqonyeni kadoti. 
(e) Akufanele kuphela ukuba ingane izame ukufunda lokho okufundiswa ekilasini, kodwa kufanele futhi ifunde ngengadi, ngokuthunga nangeminye imisebenzi yezandla. (f) Amamonitha esikoleni anemisebenzi ethile okufanele ayifeze kahle ngokwethembeka. Eminye yalemisebenzi 
194 
ukuphatha ezinye izingane, abheke ukuthi ziziphatha ngemfanelo yini njengoba kulindelekile esikoleni. Ama. monitha anokutshelwa ukuba aqaphele njalo ukuthi amabhlekibhodi esuliwe, namadeski lapho kuhleli khona abafundi ahlanzekile. Kungumsebenzi wamamonitha futhi ukubheka ukuthizonke izincwadi ziqoqiwe yini zafakwa ekhabetheni. 
AMATHUBA 
Amathuba noma inzuzo etholakala esikoleni isobala. 
Izingane zisiwa esikoleni ukuba ziyofunda ukufunda, ukubhala nokwenza izibalo; ngabantu basendulo nokuthi yini abasenzela yona. Izingane zifunda futhi ngabantu bakubo, basezweni lakubo nabakwamanye amazwe, ukuthi bahlala kanjani basebenzeni. Zifunda futhi ngemithetho esemqoka yempilo; zifunda .ukuthunga nokuchibiyela izingubo; ukutshala izilimo nezimbali, nokwenza izinto ezahlukene ngezandla. 
Izingane zifunda ngoNkulunkulu nangeBhayibheli. 
Zaziswe ukuthi uNkulunkulu ufuna ziziphathe kanjani komunye umuntu. 
  Zifundiswa ukucabanga nokwenza izinto, zazi ukuthi kufanele zikhule kanjani hayi emzimbeni nasengqondweni kuphela, kepha futhi esimilweni. 
  N gesikhathi izingane zifunda konke lokhu ziba nabangani abaningi. 
  Ngamathuba amakhulu lawa; kakuyona into okufanele siyikhohlwe ukuthi ziningi izingane ezingenawo neze. Izikole kazibanele bonke labo abafuna ukufunda. 
  Labo abethu abanethuba lokufunda kufanele bazame ngawo wonke amandla abo ukulisebenzisa ngokuphelele lelithuba. 
INDLELA ABAZAU ABAZIBHEKA NGAYO IZINGANE ZABO, NENDLELA IZINGANE OKUFANELE ZIZIPHATHE NGAYO KUBAZAU BAZO 
  Uma ukufunde kahle wakuzwisisa lokhu osekushiwo ngenhla, usubone izindlela eziningi abazali abanakelela ngazo izingane zabo. Usubone futhi nezindlela izingane okufanele ziziphathe ngazo kubazali bazo. Nantu uhlu olulandelayo:

153. 
  Abazali abahle izingane zabo bazinika ukudla, okakwembatha, babone futhi ukuthi izingane zabo zivikelekile zihlala ezindlini. Bazinika imithi noma bazise kudokotela uma zigula. Bazifundisa indlela okufanele ziziphathe ngayo uma zizodwa nalapho kukhona abantu abadala' bazifundisa indlela efanele yokudla, kanye nendlela' okugezwa kugqokwe ngayo. Bazifundisa inkolo, bazikhombise izinto ezinhle nezimbi. Bazifundisa ukuba zethembeke, zilunge, zibenesibindi futhi zibe msulwa. Bazithumela esikoleni bese kuthi ngamasonto bahambe nazo baye esontweni.      ISAHLUKO 23 KUPHEPHA EZINGOZINI 
  (Okuningi okuqukethwe yilesi sahluko kuthathwe ecwajaneni yeNational Road Safety Organisation ebizwa ngokuthi The Highway Code of South Africa. Sifisa ukuveza umbongo wethu omkhulu ngosizo esiluthole lrulencwajana.) 
A. IMITHETHO YOKUZIPHEPHISA OKUFANELE IKHUNJULWE NGABAGIBELE AMABHAYISIKILI. 
1. HAMBELA NGASESANDLENI SOBUNXELE-Ngaso sonke isikhathi uma ugibele ibhayisikili ubohambela ekupheleni komgwaqo ngakwesobunxele ukuze izimoto namalori kukwedlule ngaphandle kwengozi. 
2. GIBELANI NlLANDELANE-Uma nigibele nibabili noma ningaphezulu kwalokho nibogibela nilandelane ngakwesobunxele. Ningalokothi nigibele nilinganisane. 
3. GIBE LA UQONDE NGQO PHAMBlu-Ungalokothi ugwincize phakathi kwezimoto. Gibela uqonde ngqo phambili. Abanye bayathanda ukushona Ie nale emgwaqeni, bangene nasezikhaleni phakathi kwezimoto. Ningakwenzi lokho. 
4. UNGASHONISI IKHANDA PHANsI-Aliphakame njalo ikhanda yikhona uzobona kahle yonke into. 
5. AKUBE KRONA IBANGA ELANELE-Phakathi kwakho nalokho okuhamba phambi kwakho. Uma kwenzeka leyonto ima ungalindele. uzokwazi ukuyivika ungayishayisi.

ndlela ephephile lena yokujikela ngasesandleni sokudla uma kuphithizela kakhulu. 
(b) Uma kungaphithizeli kakhulu. 
    Qala ngokubheka emuva ubone ukuthi akukho lutho yini olunejubane elikhulu olukwedlulayo. Bese-ke wenza isiboniso ngokwelula ingalo yakho yangakwesokudla ukhombe lapho ujikela ngakhona. Suka-ke ngakwesobunxele ungenele phakathi yikhona uzothi ufika lapho imigwaqo iphambana khona bese uphakathi nomgwaqo. ]ika-ke njengoba kuboniswa emfanekisweni, . uhambele ngalena kwe 'bala' eliphakathi nendawo. 
    Uma lingekho leli bala, thatha njengokungathi likhona uhambele ngalena kwalo. Ungakhohlwa ukuqaphela izinto eziqhamuka ngakuX. 
12. Izinto ezimbalwa okufanele ungazenzi-: 
(a) Ungagibelisi muntu ebhayisikilini. Kuyingozi kabi ukugibelisana kanti futhi wukwephula umthetho. 
(b) Ungabambeleli ezomotweni nasemalorini. Kuyenzeka ukuba lomkhuba uveze izidumbu. 
(e) Ungagibeli ufake izandla ezikhwameni. Ungagibeli ubeke izinyawo zakho ezimpondweni. Uma wenze njalo uzolibamba kanjani ibhayisikili lakho? Bese-ke kuvela ingozi embi. 
(d) Ungahambi ngejubane elikhulu ekwehleleni.

a. Uma unqamula umgwaqo lapho kupendwe khona ngokumhlophe. hambela NGAKWESOBUNXELE.
